He has had more than thirty singles on the Billboard country charts, of which seven have reached number 1: \"I Love the Way You Love Me\", \"I Swear\", \"Be My Baby Tonight\", \"\"f You've Got Love\", \"I Can Love You Like That\", \"Sold\", and \"The Little Girl\". Thirteen more have reached the top 10. \"I Swear\" and \"Sold\" were named by Billboard as the top country songs of 1994 and 1995, respectively. Several of Montgomery's singles crossed over to the Billboard Hot 100, his highest peak there having been achieved by \"Letters from Home\" in 2004.","artists":[{"id":46130,"name":"John Michael
